<rate>4</rate><text>Our family is acquainted with the owner, & she said the food is gourmet Yukaton-style Mexican food. In fact, its name is a type of flowering tree that can be found on the Yukaton peninsula, hence the beautiful illuminated metal tree art on the wall by the entrance/hostess stand, & the flower tile wall behind the bar. The food is a little pricey, however, it was absolutely amazing & cooked perfectly (I got the carne asada dish), so it was totally worth it! I've only eaten here once about 3 months after they first opened though, so maybe they have since incorporated music, & perhaps there are better servers. < Text>
Random date night and just wanted to try something different in Fresno. Found this place which has only been opened for about three months. Walked in without reservation at 6:30pm-ish and was seated right away. Their menu was super simple but enough.
Got the ceviche to start. It was clean and refreshing. I got the trout and the wifey got the chicken mole. The trout was not dry and well seasoned. My wife‚Äôs chicken was actually better and wasn‚Äôt dry at all either. Overall, the food tasted great for a random place to eat out.
This place is probably not a good first date choice as it‚Äôs kinda pricy and not a good place for a romantic date as the ambience isn‚Äôt fitting. But this place is fitting for a let‚Äôs just get away from the kids.<//Text>

< text>
All Creatures Animal Hospital In Murrieta saved our bunny, Max. He is adopted and has digestive special care needs (which can be fatal if not treated within 24 hours). Our Max is an indoor, tame, affectionate, interactive family household pet who acts more like a dog than a rabbit. We love him as much as our doggies! Max is a gift to our lives and we cherish him with our entire hearts.
If it weren't for Dr.'s dedication to take all life saving measures to treat Max(our bunny) over the last 5 days, he would have perished a painful death from bloat, constipation, stopped eating/drinking. This is called GI Stasis and often cause a rabbit's death within 12 to 24 hours, even with veterinary care. We learned this almost too late with Max before we discovered Max's digestive disorder that almost lead to deadly status last year. We took him to an exotic vet specialist in San Diego who did a wonderful job treating and educating us on how to care for Max's special needs. We thought we had it under control until last Monday when none of the regular prescription medications from San Diego vet specialist stopped working for the first time. We were unable to return to the San Diego exotic vet due to costs and distance. Our financial situation is temporarily changed which broke my heart knowing our budget was too limited to fit in this level of a pet emergency. Thank goodness for finding All Creatures Vetrinary Care which also happens to be a few blocks from my home and was very affordable compared to my previous exotic vet bills(or regular vet bills from our dogs). Because Dr was very conscientious of my limited budget, he worked very hard to save me money without compromising Max's life. I have NEVER in all my years as a pet owner, young, broke, or financially secure later in my life, experienced a vet who administers lifesaving measures to a pet that are not attached to expensive fees....this causes loss of a beloved pet simply because it's unaffordable to save your fur baby in a life threatening emergency. Dr. at All Creatures cared more about my bunny's life than charging extensive fees and still worked within my limited budget...he went above and beyond what I could afford because he clearly cared about Max and our love for our special pet. I cannot express my gratitude enough and can only thank him and the staff at All Creatures Vet in Murrieta by letting others on the internet know of their kindness, skill, and dedication to save Max's life without charging me an arm and a leg to do so. Without them, Max would have perished. Thank you so much, All Creatures Animal Hospital.
monika and Max.<//text>

<user>106447710963818231100< /user><Response>None</Response><Name>Gillian Allen<//Name><rate>1< /rate><Text>I went because my cat seemed "off", throwing up small amounts of food, kinda tired. About $800 of tests later, the doctor called us on a Friday evening to tell us that our cat was very seriously ill and needed to come in first thing in the morning. We did, we were shown a lab report for a blood test with a result that was far out of normal range. The doctor's suggestion was that we board our cat in the hospital for the weekend for about $2000 and then redo the blood test on Monday morning. We said we needed to think about it and would take our cat home for the time being. We were made to feel like we were bad pet owners.

On the way out I asked for a copy of the lab report. The receptionists did not want to give this to me although they didn't actually refuse, but I made it clear that I wasn't leaving without it and I waited for about 10 minutes to get it. Here is the out of range result:

"Quantitative Platelet:  30 (L)  Reference Range 200-500
Two smears have been reviewed an a minor degree of platelet clumping is seen. This may spuriously lower the platelet count and estimate.
COMMENT
Clots are detected in the LTT. These may falsely decrease the WBC, RBC, and platelet count, and may affect the differential. For most accurate results, please resubmit a new LTT."

Some internet research later and we learned:
* a 30 result for this level would mean the cat is dead. He'd be dead if it were under about 100.
* it is very easy to clot a cat blood sample
* if you do have a clotted sample, this platelet count is likely to be very wrong.

We did not go back to All Creatures, we took our cat to Butterfield Stage Animal Hospital where they did a full exam and blood test for $55 and gave him a clean bill of health. He had an enormous hairball shortly after and is fine.< /Text>< GmapID>

We took our two dogs here to board them while we were out of town.  We have a Lab and a Cocker Spaniel. I put antibiotic ointment on it and had to soak a wash cloth and hold it on the bite every day for about two weeks and slowly the crust started to come off, until there was none left.  He finally healed.

When we had an emergency with our guinea pig, they were the only vet in town that "claimed" on their sign they were an exotic animal vet.  We went there in desperation.  We were charged a $75 emergency fee and the doctor was already there seeing another patient.
After much treatment, which I believe he did not need, my guinea pig ended up dying anyway.  I believe they never found out what the real cause of his sickness was and didn't care.  The"doctor" only wanted our money.

When the doctor asked us why we didn't bring our dogs there for boarding anymore, I told him of the bite incident.  He only said, "you should tell us".  I believe they knew about it the whole time and never bothered to tell us.

When it came time to put our Cocker Spaniel down because he was very ill, he more than gladly wanted to do it.  (For the money, not for compassion.)  Needless to say, we had already gone to Butterfield Animal Hospital where they really care!

He charges $ for a pre-vaccination exam and all he does is check their teeth for 2 seconds and he says "We need to brush his teeth".  Then he whammo gives them a shot one after the other without caring how the pet feels, or giving our pet a break in between shots.

He also doesn't care if the boardatella goes into the nose or on the floor.

< review>
I wish I could write a review that would fully describe the experience we had at this Avis location.  The words will still fall short.
We are regular renters here (we drive an Electric car so regularly rent a gas vehicle for longer drives.  Plus my spouse has a corporate account).
This weekend I went it to pick up our rental and met Regina behind the counter.  The car I was given was filthy.  There were smashed chips on the drivers side floorboard, old french fries under the seats, crumbs all over the dash and center console.  I returned immediately and informed Regina that our car was not acceptable.  She said, "I'm sorry that's all I have to give you."  I asked her to clarify and she repeated herself.  So I said, "Are you telling me that my only option is to pay $XXX for a filthy car?"  She said, "Yes."  There was no apology. No offer to locate another car at a different location.  She could have given me a discount.  She could have given me a voucher to pay for a carwash.  She did NOTHING.  I informed her that I would not be using Avis again and she just said, "OK."  I left with the car and we tried to call the 800 number, but it was already closed. We posted a review on the corporate Facebook page, and on the Facebook page for this location.  Corporate responded 24 hours later (however the location itself did not) and said our only option was to exchange the car at another location.  But by this time, we were on our trip and in the middle of the desert, far from any Avis locations.
Upon return my husband went with me to return the car.  Guess who was there?  Regina!  My husband brought up the condition of the car and how unhappy we were.  Her response was (and this is a direct quote), "Oh."  She then informed us that we had a balance due.  We most definitely did not have a balance due.  I paid the entire balance when I picked up the car up and I returned it with a full tank of gas.  I told Regina as much and she just stared at me and said, "This says you have a balance due."  She didn't check our account.  We asked her what the balance was for and she said, "I don't know."  We paid the balance, and then called the corporate number again from the parking lot.  It was at this time that we FINALLY received some help.  The helpful agent confirmed that we were indeed fraudulently overcharged.  A coupon had been removed from the original amount we owed.  She refunded us our money and offered us a $50 voucher for the inconvenience.  She also apologized.  We will give Avis another chance, but not at this location.  And I truly hope that Regina finds herself in need of employment outside of customer service.</review>

< Text>
Ok guys, sooo I was a firm believer that you should never eat food from a taco truck, boy was I wrong. This place changed my mind. Over the years, I've become a regular. I've been coming here for about 6 years now and they never disappoint. You can tell they're good by the long lines that form. It's no joke, this place is good. I like their tacos de Pescado, tacos de camaron, Shimp cocktail, campechana (that's the cocktail where they mix all sorts of seafood together), I have even had ostiones or oysters here a number of times. Lol. So the skeptic turned into a believer turned into an enthusiast. There you have it folks this place gets my undivided blessing. Now, go get yourself an appetite and order anything from this truck. It won't disappoint.</Text>

< Review>
You ever eat a burger with a fork and knife before?

I don't mean just to cut it in half, either. I mean every single glorious bite. Have you? And I'm not talking about a chili burger, which makes forks a requirement immediately. I'm talking about a huge, drippy, flavorful burger that will make you rethink where your favorite burger comes from.

Well, that burger is the Gangster burger, and it is at Falafel Corner.

Pictures don't do it justice. It is amazing from bite one to bite 50, and it is definitely something that should be on your list of things you need to try in Sacramento.

Their gyros are also splendid, and full of rich flavors that scream authentic and fresh. But that burger.

That burger. If you had told me that my favorite burger would be from a place that sells falafel, I would have laughed.

I'm not laughing now. Try it out.< /Review>

< Review>
The Gyro is decent but the platter and Hummus weren't great. I've been here twice and I would suggest going to Eat A Pita instead, it's about 10 minutes away.

One thing that really annoyed me was I got a side of Hummus and they didn't give me any bread or chips with it so I couldn't eat it. On top of that they love to drench their hummus in way too much oil and they throw so much raw spice on it that it overpowers everything. On the platter the meat I had was way too crispy and the rice was undercooked. Again, everything was hit with raw spice overpowering anything you eat.

Customer service is also lacking. I watched a woman walk up to the counter, wait 5 mins for someone, then leave since no one was helping her.

Edit: Changed this from a 2 star to a 3. The gyros are good just avoid the platters.<//Review>

< review>
This is the second time I've been here. Instead of the traditional fare associated with the restaurant's name, I decided to try a burger. I always enjoy a good burger topped with a fried egg so I decided to go with the Badmash (ganster) burger. OOOOOO MY!  It was easily one of the tastiest burgers I have ever eaten. The double patties of beef we're seasoned to perfection, the bacon, thick and juicy and the egg was a flavor explosion! Two types of cheeses, Swiss and Cheddar were plentiful and a useful topping for the fries, along with the tangy Badmash sauce. You'll need two hands and lots of napkins to eat this one folks! I'll be back.</review>

< Text>
This is the very best falafel edge my family and I have been to. The food is cooked to purchase and offered warm. The service was incredible!! The nice woman at the front welcomed us with a smile and also pleasantly took our order. I purchased the chicken platter, bacon cheddar burger, badmash (mobster) burger, a basket of curly french fries and also a six items of chicken wings. As I took a seat, I noticed the remarkably clean restaurant. Our food was ready promptly as well as it was still sizzling when it came out. Time for food discourse:3 Poultry plate- the hen plate was larger than expected. It was delicious, nonetheless I considered the rice to be a little oily. The hummus was fresh as well as it paired well with the pita bread. The chicken and also rice was kindly rubbed with tzatziki sauce. The rice was vivid, though a little drier than typical. Hamburgers- both hamburgers were juicy as well as not gamey whatsoever! It was a wonderful surprise, because the patty looked completely dry as well as boring however tasted scrumptious. The badsmash (gangster) hamburger was hugeeee. I was so happy the meat was halal so I can consume the tasty bacon in it. Though it behaved, I would have liked the bacon to be crispier. Curly french fries- the french fries were straightforward and also the portions were huge. They were delicious however standard. Buffalo wings- the wings were very little and also the sauce was method to sour. I wouldn't advise this product. Aside from a few points, my experience right here was remarkable to state the least.</Text>

This place is a hole in the wall with great food. LOVE this place. I went here for dinner by recommendation from a friend while I was doing a little getaway in Redondo beach and I absolutely loved it. We were quoted an hour for dinner and they were going to text us when the table was ready, it turned out to be just over 35 minutes. We went a little bit early (5:30pm) because I knew they didn't take reservations and assumed there would be a wait. While you are waiting you can order drinks from the bar and enjoy outside.

The staff was very attentive and friendly! I believe our server's name was Alex. They had great recommendations for food. They have a large menu - all sounded good. We went with Tofu fajitas and crab enchiladas, both were delicious with very LARGE portion size. They had sooo many good vegan and sea food options, along with your typical Mexican dishes. Their salsa was by far some of the best I have ever had.

I want them to open one in San Diego!

Pro tip: order the skinny house margarita! So yummmmy!< /Text>

< review>
A totally clasic unique experience...a well curated, historical "California Beach Culture" Museum and excellent restaurant...all-in-one.
Worth your time to drive to beautiful world class Redondo Beach. Make it a Wonderful Winter mini-vacation-for-the-day and bring your date or family...you won't regret it! As a matter of fact, you will never forget it!
Food is excellent, starting with the guacamole...fresh and not over-prepared. They let the wonderful avocado taste shine through.
Fish tacos? Perfection!!! Even the fried (by the Manager, Martine's suggestion...he should know...he has championed this establishment for over 20 years.)
The lobster quesadillas are not skimpy on the lobster. You get what you pay for.
Every detail has been well thought out...down to the passion fruit iced tea.
Full bar...everything! Liquor...wine and beer in vast selections.
Mood is set with tunes from great vintage tapes. Happiness: sound...sight...smell and taste...all here in spades!
A reservation is probably a good idea as there can be long lines...they're that good.
One of my top 10!</review>

<time>1593378877771</time><Rating>1< /Rating><Text>I understand that we are in a pandemic, but if a business cannot offer the highest level of quality and service, they shouldn't consider reopening. My husband and I went to Rivera Mexican Grill last night, the only good thing about the entire experience was we were seated immediately. Perhaps that should have been our first clue, as other restaurants in the area had over an hour wait.
The server was friendly but completely overwhelmed, under trained and uneducated about the menu. We ordered a Blue chip salad each, and I order a special Margarita with salt, and super hot-hot sauce for our chips.
What I received was a small margarita with NO salt, when I stated that was not what I order, she looked at me in a complete daze. I had to go to the bar and change out the drink myself. Still waiting for hot sauce 15-minutes in, we asked a bus-boy who brought us hot chili's right away, not exactly what we ordered but it worked. 35-minutes in we received our very warm, soggy salads and a saucer of hot-hot sauce. My husband and I looked at each other and just shook our heads. The salad was HORRIBLE! We know it's supposed to be slightly warm, but it had obviously sat under a heat lamp for much of our long wait. Looking around it was an entire room of frustrated patrons.

As soon as we got home, we were both so nauseated from the meal, it almost ruined date night.

My suggestion is if you go to another restaurant and they tell you it's a 40+ minute wait, that you should wait. Because you will wait once inside for your subpar food. I'd love to get my $60.00 back, I hope you save your money!< /Text>< Pictures>

Hubby and I have been coming here for over ten years. The service is always great and so is the food. I usually order their fish tacos or 2-item lunch (enchilada and a crispy taco). I had their chili verde recently and it was tender full of flavors.
Their burritos are hugh and wonderful. The only dish I think is just adequate is their tamales, everthing else is very good.
One note of caution, their salsa is AMAZING. So pace yourself so you have room to eat what you ordered. If we could drink it like gazpacho we would, it is so good.< /Text>

This place is great - best Mexican restaurant.  First - if it is crowded and you have to wait for a table as we did (7 of us) you can grab a drink from the bar and sit in their outdoor waiting area where you are served chips and salsa, which are great. <review>I must admit my expectations were a bit high and hopeful after all the positive reviews on fish tacos. We were visiting from out of state and this was my one chance.

The food was ok, not great. I ordered the fresh fish tacos w the charra beans and their "slaw," which cost $16.99 I believe. The fish was fresh but overall not much seasoning or flavor. I make better at home all the time by simply using lime and cilantro in the cabbage w a sriracha crema! Beans were good. Slaw was large chunks of cabbage, carrot, pepper and jicama which were fresh - but again, not much flavor, very lightly dressed.

Their salsa is good, chips too. Can't complain about the margarita either, heh. Service was very attentive and food did come pretty quickly but it was close to closing. Overall though, can't say I'd go back.<//review></record></dataset><record>
